          <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
           <p>
            All of my records have a field called "pictures". This field is an array of strings.
           </p>
           <p>
            I now want the newest 10 records where this array IS NOT empty.
           </p>
           <p>
            I've googled around, but strangely enough I haven't found much on this.
I've read into the $where option, but I was wondering how slow that is to native functions, and if there is a better solution.
           </p>
           <p>
            And even then, that does not work:
           </p>
           <pre class="lang-js prettyprint-override"><code>ME.find({$where: 'this.pictures.length &gt; 0'}).sort('-created').limit(10).execFind()
</code></pre>
           <p>
            Returns nothing. Leaving
            <code>
             this.pictures
            </code>
            without the length bit does work, but then it also returns empty records, of course.
           </p>
          </div>
          <div class="mt24 mb12">
           <div class="post-taglist d-flex gs4 gsy fd-column">
            <div class="d-flex ps-relative fw-wrap">
             <a class="post-tag" href="/questions/tagged/mongodb" rel="tag" title="show questions tagged 'mongodb'">

             </a>

             </a>

        <a name="25142571">

        <div class="answer js-answer accepted-answer" data-answerid="25142571" data-highest-scored="1" data-position-on-page="1" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="1124" id="answer-25142571" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="25142571">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="1124" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             1124
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/25142571/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             If you also have documents that don't have the key, you can use:
            </p>
            <pre><code>ME.find({ pictures: { $exists: true, $not: {$size: 0} } })
</code></pre>
            <p>
             MongoDB doesn't use indexes if
             <code>
              $size
             </code>
             is involved, so here is a better solution:
            </p>
            <pre><code>ME.find({ pictures: { $exists: true, $ne: [] } })
</code></pre>
            <p>
             If your property can have invalid values (like
             <code>
              null
             </code>
             <code>
              boolean
             </code>
             or others) , then you an add an additional check
             <a href="https://docs.mongodb.com/manual/reference/operator/query/type/" rel="noreferrer">
              using
              <code>
               $types
              </code>
             </a>
             as proposed
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/a/52465830/968799">
              in this answer
             </a>
             :
            </p>
            <p>
             With mongo &gt;= 3.2:
            </p>
            <pre><code>ME.find({ pictures: { $exists: true, $type: 'array', $ne: [] } })
</code></pre>
            <p>
             With mongo &lt; 3.2:
            </p>
            <pre><code>ME.find({ pictures: { $exists: true, $type: 4, $ne: [] } })
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Since the MongoDB 2.6 release, you can compare with the operator
             <code>
              $gt
             </code>
             , but this could lead to unexpected results (you can find a detailed explanation
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/14789684/find-mongodb-records-where-array-field-is-not-empty/42601244#42601244">
              in this answer
             </a>
             ):
            </p>
            <pre><code>ME.find({ pictures: { $gt: [] } })
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

                 To me that's the correct approach, since it makes sure the array exists and is not empty.

             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="72329348" data-comment-owner-id="1579058" data-comment-score="62" id="comment-72329348">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
               <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="supernova" title="number of 'useful comment' votes received">
                 62
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 CAREFUL,
                 <code>
                  ME.find({ pictures: { $gt: [] } })
                 </code>
                 IS DANGEROUS, even in newer MongoDB versions. If you have an index on your list field and that index is utilized during the query, you will get unexpected results. For example:
                 <code>
                  db.doc.find({'nums': { $gt: [] }}).hint({ _id: 1 }).count()
                 </code>
                 returns the right number, while
                 <code>
                  db.doc.find({'nums': { $gt: [] }}).hint({ nums: 1 }).count()
                 </code>
                 returns
                 <code>
                  0
                 </code>
                 .
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/1579058/wojcikstefan" title="837 reputation">
                  wojcikstefan
                 </a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">
                 <span class="relativetime-clean" title="2017-03-04 17:51:09Z, License: CC BY-SA 3.0">
                  Mar 4, 2017 at 17:51
                 </span>
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
             </li>
             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="72335010" data-comment-owner-id="1579058" data-comment-score="3" id="comment-72335010">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
               <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="cool" title="number of 'useful comment' votes received">
                 3
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 See my detailed answer below to learn why this might not work for you:
                 <a href="http://stackoverflow.com/a/42601244/1579058">
                  stackoverflow.com/a/42601244/1579058
                 </a>
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/1579058/wojcikstefan" title="837 reputation">
                  wojcikstefan
                 </a>
                </div>

             </li>
             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="73894062" data-comment-owner-id="119259" data-comment-score="6" id="comment-73894062">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">

                  better solution
                 </a>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             After some more looking, especially in the mongodb documents, and puzzling bits together, this was the answer:
            </p>
            <pre><code>ME.find({pictures: {$exists: true, $not: {$size: 0}}})
</code></pre>
           </div>

               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 Be careful, mongoDB won't use indexes if $size is involved
                 <a href="http://docs.mongodb.org/manual/reference/operator/query/size/" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
                  link
                 </a>
                 . Would be better to include {$ne:[]} and possibly {$ne:null}.
                </span>

                <span class="comment-copy">
                 @Cec All the documentation says is that if you use $size in the query, it won't use any index to give you faster results. So if you have an index on that field and you want to use it, stick to other approaches like {$ne:[]}, if that works for you, that will use your index.
                </span>

             This might also work for you:
            </p>
            <pre><code>ME.find({'pictures.0': {$exists: true}});

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="42601244" data-highest-scored="0" data-position-on-page="4" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="38" id="answer-42601244" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="42601244">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="38" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             38
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/42601244/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

             </svg>
            </a>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             You care about two things when querying - accuracy and performance. With that in mind, I tested a few different approaches in MongoDB v3.0.14.
            </p>
            <p>
             TL;DR
             <code>
              db.doc.find({ nums: { $gt: -Infinity }})
             </code>
             is the fastest and most reliable (at least in the MongoDB version I tested).
            </p>
            <p>
             <em>
              EDIT: This no longer works in MongoDB v3.6! See the comments under this post for a potential solution.
             </em>
            </p>
            <h3>
             Setup
            </h3>
            <p>
             I inserted 1k docs w/o a list field, 1k docs with an empty list, and 5 docs with a non-empty list.
            </p>
            <pre><code>for (var i = 0; i &lt; 1000; i++) { db.doc.insert({}); }
for (var i = 0; i &lt; 1000; i++) { db.doc.insert({ nums: [] }); }
for (var i = 0; i &lt; 5; i++) { db.doc.insert({ nums: [1, 2, 3] }); }
db.doc.createIndex({ nums: 1 });
</code></pre>
            <p>
             I recognize this isn't enough of a scale to take performance as seriously as I am in the tests below, but it's enough to present the correctness of various queries and behavior of chosen query plans.
            </p>
            <h3>
             Tests
            </h3>
            <p>
             <code>
              db.doc.find({'nums': {'$exists': true}})
             </code>
             returns wrong results (for what we're trying to accomplish).
            </p>
            <pre><code>MacBook-Pro(mongod-3.0.14) test&gt; db.doc.find({'nums': {'$exists': true}}).count()
1005
</code></pre>
            <p>
             --
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              db.doc.find({'nums.0': {'$exists': true}})
             </code>
             returns correct results, but it's also slow using a full collection scan (notice
             <code>
              COLLSCAN
             </code>
             stage in the explanation).
            </p>
            <pre><code>MacBook-Pro(mongod-3.0.14) test&gt; db.doc.find({'nums.0': {'$exists': true}}).count()
5
MacBook-Pro(mongod-3.0.14) test&gt; db.doc.find({'nums.0': {'$exists': true}}).explain()
{
  "queryPlanner": {
    "plannerVersion": 1,
    "namespace": "test.doc",
    "indexFilterSet": false,
    "parsedQuery": {
      "nums.0": {
        "$exists": true
      }
    },
    "winningPlan": {
      "stage": "COLLSCAN",
      "filter": {
        "nums.0": {
          "$exists": true
        }
      },
      "direction": "forward"
    },
    "rejectedPlans": [ ]
  },
  "serverInfo": {
    "host": "MacBook-Pro",
    "port": 27017,
    "version": "3.0.14",
    "gitVersion": "08352afcca24bfc145240a0fac9d28b978ab77f3"
  },
  "ok": 1
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             --
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              db.doc.find({'nums': { $exists: true, $gt: { '$size': 0 }}})
             </code>
             returns wrong results. That's because of an invalid index scan advancing no documents. It will likely be accurate but slow without the index.
            </p>
            <pre><code>MacBook-Pro(mongod-3.0.14) test&gt; db.doc.find({'nums': { $exists: true, $gt: { '$size': 0 }}}).count()
0
MacBook-Pro(mongod-3.0.14) test&gt; db.doc.find({'nums': { $exists: true, $gt: { '$size': 0 }}}).explain('executionStats').executionStats.executionStages
{
  "stage": "KEEP_MUTATIONS",
  "nReturned": 0,
  "executionTimeMillisEstimate": 0,
  "works": 2,
  "advanced": 0,
  "needTime": 0,
  "needFetch": 0,
  "saveState": 0,
  "restoreState": 0,
  "isEOF": 1,
  "invalidates": 0,
  "inputStage": {
    "stage": "FETCH",
    "filter": {
      "$and": [
        {
          "nums": {
            "$gt": {
              "$size": 0
            }
          }
        },
        {
          "nums": {
            "$exists": true
          }
        }
      ]
    },
    "nReturned": 0,
    "executionTimeMillisEstimate": 0,
    "works": 1,
    "advanced": 0,
    "needTime": 0,
    "needFetch": 0,
    "saveState": 0,
    "restoreState": 0,
    "isEOF": 1,
    "invalidates": 0,
    "docsExamined": 0,
    "alreadyHasObj": 0,
    "inputStage": {
      "stage": "IXSCAN",
      "nReturned": 0,
      "executionTimeMillisEstimate": 0,
      "works": 1,
      "advanced": 0,
      "needTime": 0,
      "needFetch": 0,
      "saveState": 0,
      "restoreState": 0,
      "isEOF": 1,
      "invalidates": 0,
      "keyPattern": {
        "nums": 1
      },
      "indexName": "nums_1",
      "isMultiKey": true,
      "direction": "forward",
      "indexBounds": {
        "nums": [
          "({ $size: 0.0 }, [])"
        ]
      },
      "keysExamined": 0,
      "dupsTested": 0,
      "dupsDropped": 0,
      "seenInvalidated": 0,
      "matchTested": 0
    }
  }
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             --
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              db.doc.find({'nums': { $exists: true, $not: { '$size': 0 }}})
             </code>
             returns correct results, but the performance is bad. It technically does an index scan, but then it still advances all the docs and then has to filter through them).
            </p>
            <pre><code>MacBook-Pro(mongod-3.0.14) test&gt; db.doc.find({'nums': { $exists: true, $not: { '$size': 0 }}}).count()
5
MacBook-Pro(mongod-3.0.14) test&gt; db.doc.find({'nums': { $exists: true, $not: { '$size': 0 }}}).explain('executionStats').executionStats.executionStages
{
  "stage": "KEEP_MUTATIONS",
  "nReturned": 5,
  "executionTimeMillisEstimate": 0,
  "works": 2016,
  "advanced": 5,
  "needTime": 2010,
  "needFetch": 0,
  "saveState": 15,
  "restoreState": 15,
  "isEOF": 1,
  "invalidates": 0,
  "inputStage": {
    "stage": "FETCH",
    "filter": {
      "$and": [
        {
          "nums": {
            "$exists": true
          }
        },
        {
          "$not": {
            "nums": {
              "$size": 0
            }
          }
        }
      ]
    },
    "nReturned": 5,
    "executionTimeMillisEstimate": 0,
    "works": 2016,
    "advanced": 5,
    "needTime": 2010,
    "needFetch": 0,
    "saveState": 15,
    "restoreState": 15,
    "isEOF": 1,
    "invalidates": 0,
    "docsExamined": 2005,
    "alreadyHasObj": 0,
    "inputStage": {
      "stage": "IXSCAN",
      "nReturned": 2005,
      "executionTimeMillisEstimate": 0,
      "works": 2015,
      "advanced": 2005,
      "needTime": 10,
      "needFetch": 0,
      "saveState": 15,
      "restoreState": 15,
      "isEOF": 1,
      "invalidates": 0,
      "keyPattern": {
        "nums": 1
      },
      "indexName": "nums_1",
      "isMultiKey": true,
      "direction": "forward",
      "indexBounds": {
        "nums": [
          "[MinKey, MaxKey]"
        ]
      },
      "keysExamined": 2015,
      "dupsTested": 2015,
      "dupsDropped": 10,
      "seenInvalidated": 0,
      "matchTested": 0
    }
  }
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             --
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              db.doc.find({'nums': { $exists: true, $ne: [] }})
             </code>
             returns correct results and is slightly faster, but the performance is still not ideal. It uses IXSCAN which only advances docs with an existing list field, but then has to filter out the empty lists one by one.
            </p>
            <pre><code>MacBook-Pro(mongod-3.0.14) test&gt; db.doc.find({'nums': { $exists: true, $ne: [] }}).count()
5
MacBook-Pro(mongod-3.0.14) test&gt; db.doc.find({'nums': { $exists: true, $ne: [] }}).explain('executionStats').executionStats.executionStages
{
  "stage": "KEEP_MUTATIONS",
  "nReturned": 5,
  "executionTimeMillisEstimate": 0,
  "works": 1018,
  "advanced": 5,
  "needTime": 1011,
  "needFetch": 0,
  "saveState": 15,
  "restoreState": 15,
  "isEOF": 1,
  "invalidates": 0,
  "inputStage": {
    "stage": "FETCH",
    "filter": {
      "$and": [
        {
          "$not": {
            "nums": {
              "$eq": [ ]
            }
          }
        },
        {
          "nums": {
            "$exists": true
          }
        }
      ]
    },
    "nReturned": 5,
    "executionTimeMillisEstimate": 0,
    "works": 1017,
    "advanced": 5,
    "needTime": 1011,
    "needFetch": 0,
    "saveState": 15,
    "restoreState": 15,
    "isEOF": 1,
    "invalidates": 0,
    "docsExamined": 1005,
    "alreadyHasObj": 0,
    "inputStage": {
      "stage": "IXSCAN",
      "nReturned": 1005,
      "executionTimeMillisEstimate": 0,
      "works": 1016,
      "advanced": 1005,
      "needTime": 11,
      "needFetch": 0,
      "saveState": 15,
      "restoreState": 15,
      "isEOF": 1,
      "invalidates": 0,
      "keyPattern": {
        "nums": 1
      },
      "indexName": "nums_1",
      "isMultiKey": true,
      "direction": "forward",
      "indexBounds": {
        "nums": [
          "[MinKey, undefined)",
          "(undefined, [])",
          "([], MaxKey]"
        ]
      },
      "keysExamined": 1016,
      "dupsTested": 1015,
      "dupsDropped": 10,
      "seenInvalidated": 0,
      "matchTested": 0
    }
  }
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             --
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              db.doc.find({'nums': { $gt: [] }})
             </code>
             IS DANGEROUS BECAUSE DEPENDING ON THE INDEX USED IT MIGHT GIVE UNEXPECTED RESULTS. That's because of an invalid index scan which advances no documents.
            </p>
            <pre><code>MacBook-Pro(mongod-3.0.14) test&gt; db.doc.find({'nums': { $gt: [] }}).count()
0
MacBook-Pro(mongod-3.0.14) test&gt; db.doc.find({'nums': { $gt: [] }}).hint({ nums: 1 }).count()
0
MacBook-Pro(mongod-3.0.14) test&gt; db.doc.find({'nums': { $gt: [] }}).hint({ _id: 1 }).count()
5

MacBook-Pro(mongod-3.0.14) test&gt; db.doc.find({'nums': { $gt: [] }}).explain('executionStats').executionStats.executionStages
{
  "stage": "KEEP_MUTATIONS",
  "nReturned": 0,
  "executionTimeMillisEstimate": 0,
  "works": 1,
  "advanced": 0,
  "needTime": 0,
  "needFetch": 0,
  "saveState": 0,
  "restoreState": 0,
  "isEOF": 1,
  "invalidates": 0,
  "inputStage": {
    "stage": "FETCH",
    "filter": {
      "nums": {
        "$gt": [ ]
      }
    },
    "nReturned": 0,
    "executionTimeMillisEstimate": 0,
    "works": 1,
    "advanced": 0,
    "needTime": 0,
    "needFetch": 0,
    "saveState": 0,
    "restoreState": 0,
    "isEOF": 1,
    "invalidates": 0,
    "docsExamined": 0,
    "alreadyHasObj": 0,
    "inputStage": {
      "stage": "IXSCAN",
      "nReturned": 0,
      "executionTimeMillisEstimate": 0,
      "works": 1,
      "advanced": 0,
      "needTime": 0,
      "needFetch": 0,
      "saveState": 0,
      "restoreState": 0,
      "isEOF": 1,
      "invalidates": 0,
      "keyPattern": {
        "nums": 1
      },
      "indexName": "nums_1",
      "isMultiKey": true,
      "direction": "forward",
      "indexBounds": {
        "nums": [
          "([], BinData(0, ))"
        ]
      },
      "keysExamined": 0,
      "dupsTested": 0,
      "dupsDropped": 0,
      "seenInvalidated": 0,
      "matchTested": 0
    }
  }
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             --
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              db.doc.find({'nums.0’: { $gt: -Infinity }})
             </code>
             returns correct results, but has bad performance (uses a full collection scan).
            </p>
            <pre><code>MacBook-Pro(mongod-3.0.14) test&gt; db.doc.find({'nums.0': { $gt: -Infinity }}).count()
5
MacBook-Pro(mongod-3.0.14) test&gt; db.doc.find({'nums.0': { $gt: -Infinity }}).explain('executionStats').executionStats.executionStages
{
  "stage": "COLLSCAN",
  "filter": {
    "nums.0": {
      "$gt": -Infinity
    }
  },
  "nReturned": 5,
  "executionTimeMillisEstimate": 0,
  "works": 2007,
  "advanced": 5,
  "needTime": 2001,
  "needFetch": 0,
  "saveState": 15,
  "restoreState": 15,
  "isEOF": 1,
  "invalidates": 0,
  "direction": "forward",
  "docsExamined": 2005
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             --
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              db.doc.find({'nums': { $gt: -Infinity }})
             </code>
             surprisingly, this works very well! It gives the right results and it's fast, advancing 5 docs from the index scan phase.
            </p>
            <pre><code>MacBook-Pro(mongod-3.0.14) test&gt; db.doc.find({'nums': { $gt: -Infinity }}).explain('executionStats').executionStats.executionStages
{
  "stage": "FETCH",
  "nReturned": 5,
  "executionTimeMillisEstimate": 0,
  "works": 16,
  "advanced": 5,
  "needTime": 10,
  "needFetch": 0,
  "saveState": 0,
  "restoreState": 0,
  "isEOF": 1,
  "invalidates": 0,
  "docsExamined": 5,
  "alreadyHasObj": 0,
  "inputStage": {
    "stage": "IXSCAN",
    "nReturned": 5,
    "executionTimeMillisEstimate": 0,
    "works": 15,
    "advanced": 5,
    "needTime": 10,
    "needFetch": 0,
    "saveState": 0,
    "restoreState": 0,
    "isEOF": 1,
    "invalidates": 0,
    "keyPattern": {
      "nums": 1
    },
    "indexName": "nums_1",
    "isMultiKey": true,
    "direction": "forward",
    "indexBounds": {
      "nums": [
        "(-inf.0, inf.0]"
      ]
    },
    "keysExamined": 15,
    "dupsTested": 15,
    "dupsDropped": 10,
    "seenInvalidated": 0,
    "matchTested": 0
  }
}
</code></pre>

                <span class="comment-copy">
                 Thanks for your very detailed answer @wojcikstefan. Unfortunately, your suggested solution doesn't seem to work in my case. I have a MongoDB 3.6.4 collection with 2m documents, most of them having a
                 <code>
                  seen_events
                 </code>
                 String array, which is also indexed.  Searching with
                 <code>
                  { $gt: -Infinity }
                 </code>
                 , I immediately get 0 documents. Using
                 <code>
                  { $exists: true, $ne: [] }
                 </code>
                 I get the more likely 1,2m docs, with a lot of time being wasted in the FETCH stage:
                 <a href="https://gist.github.com/N-Coder/b9e89a925e895c605d84bfeed648d82c" rel="nofollow noreferrer">

             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="87759160" data-comment-owner-id="1579058" data-comment-score="0" id="comment-87759160">

               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 It seems that you're right @Ncode - this no longer works in MongoDB v3.6 :( I played around with it for a few minutes and here's what I found: 1.
                 <code>
                  db.test_collection.find({"seen_events.0": {$exists: true}})
                 </code>
                 is bad because it uses a collection scan. 2.
                 <code>
                  db.test_collection.find({seen_events: {$exists: true, $ne: []}})
                 </code>
                 is bad because its IXSCAN matches all documents and then the filtering is performed in the slow FETCH phase. 3. Same goes for
                 <code>
                  db.test_collection.find({seen_events: {$exists: true, $not: {$size: 0}}})
                 </code>
                 . 4. All the other queries return invalid results.
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/1579058/wojcikstefan" title="837 reputation">
                  wojcikstefan

              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 @NCode found a solution! If you're certain that all non-empty
                 <code>
                  seen_events
                 </code>
                 contain strings, you can use this:
                 <code>
                  db.test_collection.find({seen_events: {$gt: ''}}).count()
                 </code>
                 . To confirm it performs well, check out
                 <code>
                  db.test_collection.find({seen_events: {$gt: ''}}).explain(true).executionStats
                 </code>
                 . You can probably
                 <i>
                  enforce
                 </i>
                 that seen events are strings via schema validation:
                 <a href="https://docs.mongodb.com/manual/core/schema-validation/" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
                  docs.mongodb.com/manual/core/schema-validation
                 </a>
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="28368768" data-highest-scored="0" data-position-on-page="5" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="32" id="answer-28368768" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="28368768">

             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/28368768/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Starting with the 2.6 release, another way to do this is to compare the field to an empty array:
            </p>
            <pre class="lang-javascript prettyprint-override"><code>ME.find({pictures: {$gt: []}})
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Testing it out in the shell:
            </p>
            <pre class="lang-javascript prettyprint-override"><code>&gt; db.ME.insert([
{pictures: [1,2,3]},
{pictures: []},
{pictures: ['']},
{pictures: [0]},
{pictures: 1},
{foobar: 1}
])

&gt; db.ME.find({pictures: {$gt: []}})
{ "_id": ObjectId("54d4d9ff96340090b6c1c4a7"), "pictures": [ 1, 2, 3 ] }
{ "_id": ObjectId("54d4d9ff96340090b6c1c4a9"), "pictures": [ "" ] }
{ "_id": ObjectId("54d4d9ff96340090b6c1c4aa"), "pictures": [ 0 ] }
</code></pre>
            <p>
             So it properly includes the docs where
             <code>
              pictures
             </code>
             has at least one array element, and excludes the docs where
             <code>
              pictures
             </code>
             is either an empty array, not an array, or missing.
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
             <time datetime="2015-02-06T15:10:19" itemprop="dateCreated">
             </time>

                <span class="comment-copy">
                 CAREFUL this answer might give you trouble if you try to use indexes. Doing
                 <code>
                  db.ME.createIndex({ pictures: 1 })
                 </code>
                 and then
                 <code>
                  db.ME.find({pictures: {$gt: []}})
                 </code>
                 will return zero results, at least in MongoDB v3.0.14
                </span>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="52465830" data-highest-scored="0" data-position-on-page="6" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="13" id="answer-52465830" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="52465830">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="13" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             13
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">

             </svg>

            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/52465830/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <h3>
             Retrieve all and only the documents where 'pictures' is an array and is not empty
            </h3>
            <pre><code>ME.find({pictures: {$type: 'array', $ne: []}})
</code></pre>
            <p>
             If using a MongoDb version prior to
             <a href="https://docs.mongodb.com/v3.2/reference/operator/query/type/" rel="noreferrer">
              3.2
             </a>
             , use
             <code>
              $type: 4
             </code>
             instead of
             <code>
              $type: 'array'
             </code>
             . Notice that this solution doesn't even use
             <a href="https://docs.mongodb.com/manual/reference/operator/query/size/" rel="noreferrer">
              $size
             </a>
             , so there's no problem with indexes ("Queries cannot use indexes for the $size portion of a query")
            </p>
            <p>
             Other solutions, including these (accepted answer):
            </p>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              ME.find({ pictures: { $exists: true, $not: {$size: 0} } });
  ME.find({ pictures: { $exists: true, $ne: [] } })
             </p>
            </blockquote>
            <p>
             are
             <strong>
              wrong
             </strong>
             because they return documents even if, for example, 'pictures' is
             <code>
              null
             </code>
             ,
             <code>
              undefined
             </code>
             , 0, etc.
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="30840535" data-highest-scored="0" data-position-on-page="7" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="6" id="answer-30840535" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="30840535">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="6" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             6
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/30840535/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             You can use any of the following to achieve this.
             <br/>
             Both also take care of not returning a result for objects that don't have the requested key in them:
            </p>
            <pre><code>db.video.find({pictures: {$exists: true, $gt: {$size: 0}}})
db.video.find({comments: {$exists: true, $not: {$size: 0}}})
</code></pre>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="65131401" data-highest-scored="0" data-position-on-page="8" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="4" id="answer-65131401" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="65131401">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="4" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             4
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

              </path>
             </svg>

            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/65131401/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <pre><code>db.find({ pictures: { $elemMatch: { $exists: true } } })
</code></pre>
            <p>
             <code>
              $elemMatch
             </code>
             matches documents that contain an array field with at least one element that matches the specified query.
            </p>
            <p>
             So you're matching all arrays with at least an element.
            </p>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="56211838" data-highest-scored="0" data-position-on-page="9" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="3" id="answer-56211838" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="56211838">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="3" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             3
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/56211838/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Use the
             <code>
              $elemMatch
             </code>
             operator: according to the documentation
            </p>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              The $elemMatch operator matches documents that contain an array field with at least one element that matches all the specified query criteria.
             </p>
            </blockquote>
            <p>
             <code>
              $elemMatches
             </code>
             makes sure that the value is an array and that it is not empty. So the query would be something like
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              ME.find({ pictures: { $elemMatch: {$exists: true }}})
             </code>
            </p>
            <p>
             PS A variant of this code is found in MongoDB University's M121 course.
            </p>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="35324209" data-highest-scored="0" data-position-on-page="10" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="0" id="answer-35324209" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="35324209">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

             0
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

              </path>
             </svg>

               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>

             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/35324209/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             You can also use the helper method
             <a href="http://mongoosejs.com/docs/api.html#query_Query-exists" rel="nofollow">
              Exists
             </a>
             over the Mongo operator $exists
            </p>
            <pre><code>ME.find()
    .exists('pictures')
    .where('pictures').ne([])
    .sort('-created')
    .limit(10)
    .exec(function(err, results){
        ...
    });
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
             <time datetime="2016-02-10T19:28:01" itemprop="dateCreated">

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="49023096">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

               </path>

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/49023096/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">

              </path>
             </svg>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <pre><code>{ $where: "this.pictures.length &gt; 1" }
</code></pre>
            <p>
             use the $where and pass the this.field_name.length which return the size of array field and check it by comparing with  number. if any array have any value than array size must be at least 1. so  all the array field have  length more than one, it means it have some data in that array
            </p>
           </div>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <pre><code>ME.find({pictures: {$exists: true}}) 
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Simple as that, this worked for me.
            </p>
